Ensure UnicodeRange bits are properly set.

Check ID: <FontBakeryCheck:com.google.fonts/check/unicode_range_bits>
‚ö†Ô∏è output/Noto Looped Thai/unhinted/ttf/NotoLoopedThai-Black.ttf
  • ‚ö†Ô∏è WARN

    UnicodeRange bit 0 "Basic Latin" should be 1 because cmap has 20 of the 128 codepoints in this range. [code: bad-range-bit]

  • ‚ö†Ô∏è WARN

    UnicodeRange bit 1 "Latin-1 Supplement" should be 1 because cmap has 4 of the 128 codepoints in this range. [code: bad-range-bit]

  • ‚ö†Ô∏è WARN

    UnicodeRange bit 5 "Spacing Modifier Letters" should be 1 because cmap has 2 of the 112 codepoints in this range. [code: bad-range-bit]

  • ‚ö†Ô∏è WARN

    UnicodeRange bit 6 "Combining Diacritical Marks" should be 1 because cmap has 4 of the 176 codepoints in this range. [code: bad-range-bit]

  • ‚ö†Ô∏è WARN

    UnicodeRange bit 31 "General Punctuation" should be 1 because cmap has 17 of the 240 codepoints in this range. [code: bad-range-bit]

  • ‚ö†Ô∏è WARN

    UnicodeRange bit 45 "Geometric Shapes" should be 1 because cmap has 1 of the 96 codepoints in this range. [code: bad-range-bit]

  • ‚ö†Ô∏è WARN

    UnicodeRange bit 46 "Miscellaneous Symbols" should be 1 because cmap has 1 of the 256 codepoints in this range. [code: bad-range-bit]

  • ‚ö†Ô∏è WARN

    UnicodeRange bit 60 "Private Use Area (plane 0)" should be 1 because cmap has 10 of the 6400 codepoints in this range. [code: bad-range-bit]

  • ‚ö†Ô∏è WARN

    UnicodeRange bit 80 "Khmer" should be 1 because cmap has 2 of the 160 codepoints in this range. [code: bad-range-bit]
